IMPLEMENTATION OF TEACHING AND LEARNING (T&L) ONLINE ON 29 OCTOBER 2024 UNTIL 30 OCTOBER 2024 IN CELEBRATION OF DEEPAVALI


Referring to Academic Circular No. 2/2024 dated 2 April 2024, which outlines the UTM Academic Calendar Session 2024/2025 for both Undergraduate and Postgraduate students, along with Guidelines On Exemption From Lectures During Public/Festive Holidays, as well as Online Learning Procedures (Academic Circular No. 3/2023 dated 7 August 2023), the public holiday for the Deepavali celebration on 31 October 2024 (Thursday) falls within the lecture session week.

Considering students' need to return to their hometowns for the celebration of Deepavali, the management of the Faculty of Mechanical Engineering has agreed that all Teaching and Learning (T&L) activities from 29 October 2024 (Tuesday) until 30 October 2024 (Wednesday) to be conducted virtually (online). All academic activities related to laboratories, studios, tests, and others that require physical presence will be rescheduled.

If there are students who require additional days off from classes, they can discuss this with the relevant lecturers. Consideration will be based on the needs and agreement of all parties involved.

Nevertheless, the execution of service courses involving faculties such as the *Faculty of Electrical Engineering (FKE), the Faculty of Science (FS), and the Faculty of Social Sciences and Humanities (FSSH)* is at the discretion of the respective lecturer.
Thank you.


From,
Academic Office
Faculty of Mechanical Engineering โ<This message was edited>
